or &#34;Sanuwave&#8221;) (OTCQB&#58; SNWV), a leading provider of next-generation FDA-approved wound care products, </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:174%">is pleased to provide its financial results for the three months ended September&#160;30, 2024. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:174%">Q3 2024 ended September&#160;30, 2024</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:174%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:174%;padding-left:14.5pt">Revenue for the three months ended September&#160;30, 2024, totaled $9.4 million, an increase of 89%, as compared to $5.0 million for the same period of 2023.  This growth is greater than the previously provided guidance for a 65 &#8211; 75% increase. </font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:174%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:174%;padding-left:14.5pt">124 UltraMist&#174; systems were sold in Q3 2024 up from 55 in Q3 2023 and from 72 in Q2 2024. </font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:174%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:174%;padding-left:14.5pt">UltraMist&#174; consumables revenue increased by 75% to $5.4 million (58% of revenues) in Q3 2024, versus $3.1 million for the same quarter last year. UltraMIST systems and consumables remained the primary revenue growth driver and continued to represent over 97% of SANUWAVE&#8217;s overall revenues in Q3 2024. </font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:174%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:174%;padding-left:14.5pt">Gross margin as a percentage of revenue amounted to 75.5% for the three months ended September&#160;30, 2024, versus 71.5% for the same period last year.</font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:174%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:174%;padding-left:14.5pt">For the three months ended September&#160;30, 2024, operating income totaled $2.0 million, an increase of $2.5 million compared to Q3 2023 as a result of the Company&#8217;s continued efforts to drive profitable growth and manage expenses. </font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:174%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:174%;padding-left:14.5pt">Net loss for the third quarter of 2024 was $20.7 million, driven predominantly by the change in the fair value of derivative liabilities.  This compares to a net loss of $23.7 million in the third quarter of 2023.  Net loss year to date was $18.6 million versus a net loss of $44.0 million in the nine months ended September&#160;30, 2023.</font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:174%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:174%;padding-left:14.5pt">Adjusted EBITDA </font><font style="color:#0000ff;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:174%">&#91;1&#93;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:174%"> for the three months ended September&#160;30, 2024, was $2.1 million versus Adjusted EBITDA of $(0.3) million for the same period last year, an improvement of $2.4 million.  Year to date Adjusted EBITDA was $3.5 million versus a loss of $1.8 million in the prior year period.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:174%">&#8220;The third quarter showed acceleration in revenue growth rate from the first half of the year with growth of 89% year on year (and 31% sequentially) leading the company to a growth rate of 68% for the first nine months of 2024 as compared to the same period in 2023,&#8221; said Morgan Frank, CEO.  &#8220;Obviously, we&#8217;re very pleased with these results, especially to have achieved operating income and Adjusted EBITDA positivity again this quarter and, for the first time, became cash </font></div><div style="height:45pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div><font><br></font></div></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div style="min-height:45pt;width:100%"><div><font><br></font></div></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:174%">generative from operations even after cash interest expense.  We have begun to gain traction with some larger customers and our sales funnel remains the most promising it has ever been.  As we look to the fourth quarter, we will seek to build on this progress as we continue to hire additional sales and commercial staff.  We expect to experience a bit of a &#8220;pigs through a python&#8221; scenario for us over the coming months and quarters, as large orders move the needle on revenues in significant and variable fashion, but we anticipate finishing 2024 strongly as a breakout year for Sanuwave.&#8221;</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:174%">Financial Outlook </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:174%">The Company forecasts Q4 2024 revenue of $9.7 to $10.5 million (40-50% increase from Q4 2023) and therefore for revenues for 2024 as a whole to be in excess of $32 million (an increase of 57% vs full year 2023).</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:174%">The Company forecasts Q4 gross margin as a percentage of revenue to remain in the mid-70s.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:174%">Subsequent to quarter end, the Company effected a 1-for-375 reverse stock split on October 18, 2024, completed its note and warrant exchange, and raised $10.3 million in a private placement, simplifying the Company&#8217;s capital structure and leaving it with approximately 8.5 million shares outstanding.  Details of this transaction can be found on the Sanuwave website </font><font style="color:#0e32e1;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:174%">https&#58;&#47;&#47;sanuwave.com&#47;investors&#47;press-release-details&#63;newsId&#61;OxzYFl0t620enXp1VyUG</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:174%"> or in its filings with the SEC.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:174%">As previously announced, a business update will occur via conference call on November 8, 2024 at 8&#58;30 a.m. EST. Refer to &#8220;Non-GAAP Financial Measures&#8221; and the reconciliations in this release for further information.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="height:45pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div><font><br></font></div></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div style="min-height:45pt;width:100%"><div><font><br></font></div></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:174%">About SANUWAVE</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:174%">SANUWAVE Health is focused on the research, development, and commercialization of its patented, non-invasive and biological response-activating medical systems for the repair and regeneration of skin, musculoskeletal tissue, and vascular structures.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:174%">SANUWAVE's end-to-end wound care portfolio of regenerative medicine products and product candidates helps restore the body&#8217;s normal healing processes. SANUWAVE applies and researches its patented energy transfer technologies in wound healing, orthopedic&#47;spine, aesthetic&#47;cosmetic, and cardiac&#47;endovascular conditions.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:174%">Non-GAAP Financial Measures </font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:174%">This press release includes certain financial measures that are not presented in our financial statements prepared in accordance with accounting principles generally accepted in the United States (&#8220;U.S. GAAP&#8221;). These financial measures are considered &#34;non-GAAP financial measures&#34; and are intended to supplement, and should not be considered as superior to, or a replacement for, financial measures presented in accordance with U.S. GAAP. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:174%">The Company uses Earnings Before Interest, Taxes, Depreciation and Amortization (&#8220;EBITDA&#8221;) and Adjusted EBITDA to assess its operating performance. Adjusted EBITDA is Earnings before Interest, Taxes, Depreciation and Amortization adjusted for the change in fair value of derivatives and any significant non-cash or infrequent charges.  EBITDA and Adjusted EBITDA should not be considered as alternatives to net income (loss) as a measure of financial performance or any other performance measure derived in accordance with U.S. GAAP, and they should not be construed as an inference that the Company&#8217;s future results will be unaffected by unusual or infrequent items. These non-GAAP financial measures are presented in a consistent manner for each period, unless otherwise disclosed. The Company uses these measures for the purpose of evaluating its historical and prospective financial performance, as well as its performance relative to competitors. These measures also help the Company to make operational and strategic decisions. The Company believes that providing this information to investors, in addition to U.S. GAAP measures, allows them to see the Company&#8217;s results through the eyes of management, and to better understand its historical and future financial performance. These non-GAAP financial measures are also frequently used by analysts, investors, and other interested parties to evaluate companies in our industry, when considered alongside other U.S. GAAP measures.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:174%">EBITDA and Adjusted EBITDA have their limitations as analytical tools, and you should not consider them in isolation or as a substitute for analysis of the Company&#8217;s results as reported under U.S. GAAP. Some of these limitations are that EBITDA and Adjusted EBITDA&#58;</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:174%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:174%;padding-left:14.5pt">Do not reflect every expenditure, future requirements for capital expenditures or contractual commitments.</font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:174%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:174%;padding-left:14.5pt">Do not reflect all changes in our working capital needs.</font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:174%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:174%;padding-left:14.5pt">Do not reflect interest expense, or the amount necessary to service our outstanding debt.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:174%">As presented in the U.S. GAAP to Non-GAAP Reconciliations section below, the Company&#8217;s non-GAAP financial measures exclude the impact of certain charges that contribute to our net income (loss).</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="height:45pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div><font><br></font></div></div></div><hr
